# How to Roll

Roll a d10 and a d100, minus 1 from the d10.

The d10 is the 100s place and the d100 is the tens and ones.

E.g. if you roll a 10 (-1) and a 56 that's 396.

If you roll a 1 (-1) and a 04 that's 4.

1 (-1) and a 00 becomes 1000.

# Loot Chart

#1

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Epic
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Neutral
- Passive: Extra Gear Slots
    - Gain 4 extra Gear Slots of your choice.
- Essence Value: 5000
- Credit Value: 500
- Aesthetic: Cortez (Western)

#2

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Epic
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Blue
- Passive: Resist Effects
    - Whenever you or anyone within 5 tiles of you is pushed or pulled you may reduce it by 7 tiles.
    - Once per turn you may heal up to 6 stacks of any Status Effect (may be split up any way you'd like).
- Essence Value: 5000
- Credit Value: 500
- Aesthetic: Pbosh (Viking/Heavy, Rough Metal)

#3

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Epic
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Gray
- Passive: Gray Buff
    - G = The amount of Gray pieces of gear you have equipped.
    - Perception: Gx1.25
    - Hacking: Gx1.25
    - Luck: +4
    - HP: Gx1.75
    - Group XP Gain: 4
- Essence Value: 5000
- Credit Value: 500
- Aesthetic: Jiyyagan (Survivor/Jungle)

#4

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Epic
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Red
- Passive: Damage Buff
    - Twice per turn when you hit with an attack you may raise the Tier of the Damage Dice twice.
- Essence Value: 5000
- Credit Value: 500
- Aesthetic: Jiyyagan (Survivor/Jungle)

#5

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Epic
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Gray
- Passive: Opportunity Attack
    - Up to twice per round when an enemy leaves your melee range you may target them with a free weapon attack that gets a +4 Attack Plus and +4 Damage Plus.
    - If you hit you can choose to make them stop in their tracks, wasting all their Movement Speed, or you may choose to move them up to 5 tiles in any direction.
- Essence Value: 5000
- Credit Value: 500
- Aesthetic: Ydilikian (Medieval)

#6

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Epic
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Blue
- Passive: Environmental Damage
    - When you cause a target to fall, you can make the target take 2d8 of damage per tile it falls. You may deal a d12 of damage per tile a target travels when you push or pull them against a wall or hard surface.
- Essence Value: 5000
- Credit Value: 500
- Aesthetic: Asticarian (Modern)

#7

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Epic
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Neutral
- Passive: Shortcuts
    - Spend:
    - 250 Essence to return to your home node even without clearing the node
    - 250 Essence to drop a marker, allowing you to warp back to that node even if it's within a secure sector
    - 100 Essence to get a small preview of what the next node is like
- Essence Value: 5000
- Credit Value: 500
- Aesthetic: Rtolkan (Steampunk)

- Aesthetic: Pbosh (Viking/Heavy, Rough Metal)
